WE theorised that this increased uptake of parents_highest_educ > than uptake
as compared to mother_highest_education and father_highest_education was 
because most PG mothers and fathers would get married. However, the numbers show
that only a minority of PG fathers get married to PG Mothers, whilst the majority of 
PG mothers get married to a PG father. 

Thus, considering parents_highest_education, there are (487 + 125 - 74 = 536) instances
of non double PG parents and only 74 instances of PG-PG parents. when comparing this 
to our plot of uptake stratified by both mother's and father's education. We see that:

1. There is a marked increase in the uptake of the covid vaccine with increasing income for
families where the highest is a PG (most likely father too)
and this is supported by how the slopes for father = PG in our stratified plots are much higher

2. This increase is likely not due to the pairing of PGPG parents resulting directly in 
higher income as the number of those individuals is miniscule.

We can justify that PG modifies the effect between income and uptake as compared to other
education elvels






 ^ObpLRUmG

Proposed effect:
HAving either parent be postgrad increases the rate of uptake ^mmKApWwR


So, to remove both mother and father's ed, we have to conclude that only the
highest educational level actually matters, but evidently, with the same fathers ed
changing mothers ed still changes uptake ^cUZvHBON

increase ^D0oOTp4o

increase ^SAVFJ1hc

decrease ^20NMvHMb

or actually, without the green outlier it would hold true ^H5XK75uB

For influenza, it seems that the increase in uptake only exists due to an interaction of BOTH the mother's and 
fther's highest education with income. As evidenced by how the slope is much greater.for PG PG vs X - PG or PG -X ^4OSx0T9N

Interestingly for both Covid and Influenza, there seems to be an interaction with JCTC - JCTC Parents
and income, where the uptake of influenza and covid decrease with increasing incomes, as opposed to increasing. 
with other combinations of education ^kaJqESbS
